25:T41b1,<entryFree id="n5925" key="جَعَلَ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">جَعَلَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">جعل</orth>
                  </form>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">جَعَلَ</orth>
                  </form>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">جَعْلٌ</foreign> (S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">جُعْلٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جَعَالَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جِعَالَةٌ</foreign> (K) and <foreign lang="ar">مَجْعَلٌ</foreign>, (S, TA,) <hi rend="ital">He made</hi> a thing; syn. <foreign lang="ar">صَنَعَ</foreign>; (Msb, K;) but having a more general signification than <foreign lang="ar">فَعَلَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">صَنَعَ</foreign> and their equivalents [as will be shown by what follows]; (Er-Rághib, TA;) and so   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n5925-1" target="اجتعل" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n5928"/></foreign>: (K:) both these verbs signify the same. (S.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He made</hi> a thing of, or from, a thing; as in the saying [in the Kur xvi. 74 and xlii. 9], <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنْ أَنْفُسِكُمْ أَزْوَاجًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He hath made for you, of,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">from, yourselves, wives</hi>]; and [in the Kur xvi. 83] <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الجِبَالِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَكْنَانًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And He hath made for you, of the mountains, places of retreat;</hi> as caves, and excavated houses or chambers: so explained by Bd]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He created;</hi> (K, TA;) <hi rend="ital">brought into being,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">existence;</hi> (TA;) as in the saying [in the Kur vi. 1], <foreign lang="ar">وَچَعَلَ الظُّلُمَاتِ وَالنُّورِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And hath created,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">brought into being, the darknesses and the light</hi>]; (K, TA;) and [in the Kur xxi. 31] <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلْنَا مِنَ المَآءِ كُلَّ شَىْءٍ حَىٍّ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And We have created of water,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the seminal fluid, everything living</hi>]; and [in the Kur xvi. 80, &amp;c.,] <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">لَكُمُ السَّمْعَ وَ الأَبْصَارَ وَالأَفْئِدَةَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And He created for you the ears and the eyes and the hearts</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He made,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">prepared;</hi> as in the saying [in the Kur lxv. 2], <foreign lang="ar">يَجْعَلُ لَهُ مَخْرَجًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He will make,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">prepare, for him a way of escape,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">safety</hi>]; and [in the Kur lxv. 4] <foreign lang="ar">يَجْعَلُ لَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ يُسْرًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He will make,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">prepare, for him an easy state of his circumstances;</hi> i. e., <hi rend="ital">will make his circumstances,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">case, easy to him</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He made;</hi> meaning <hi rend="ital">he made to be,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">become; he constituted; he appointed;</hi> [in which sense it is doubly trans.;] (S, K;) as in the saying in the Kur [xix. 31], <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلْنِى نَبِيًّا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And He hath made me a prophet</hi>]; (S;) [and in the elliptical phrase, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَهُ عَلَيْهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He made him to be</hi> superintendant, or the like, <hi rend="ital">over it; set him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">appointed him, over it:</hi>] and in the phrase, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَ القَبِيحَ حَسَنًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He made that which was bad to be,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">become, good</hi>]. (K.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He made</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">to be in a particular state or condition;</hi> as in the saying [in the Kur ii. 20], <foreign lang="ar">الَّذِ جَعَلَ لَكُمُ الأَرْضَ فِرَاشًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Who hath made for you the earth to be as a bed</hi>]; and [in the Kur lxxi. 15] <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلَ القَمَرَ فِيهِنَّ نُورًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And hath made the moon, in them</hi> (the heavens), <hi rend="ital">to be as a light</hi>]; and so, as some say, in the saying [in the Kur xliii. 2], <foreign lang="ar">إِنَّا جَعَلْنَاهُ قُرْآنًا عَرَبِيًّا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Verily we have made it an Arabic Kur-án</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  [<hi rend="ital">He made</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">to be in an altered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">changed, state</hi> or <hi rend="ital">condition;</hi> i. e.,] the verb signifies also the changing a thing from its state or condition; as in the saying [in the Kur xi. 84 and xv. 74], <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلْنَا عَالِيَهَا سَافِلَهَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">We made their upper part to be their lower part</hi>]; (K;) and in the words of the Kur [lvi. 81], <foreign lang="ar">وَتَجْعَلُونَ رِزْقَكُمْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَنَّكُمْ تُكَذِّبُونَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And do ye make</hi> the thanks that ye should render for <hi rend="ital">your sustenance to be that ye charge with falsehood</hi> the Giver thereof by attributing it to the stars called <foreign lang="ar">أَنْوَآء</foreign> as expl. by Bd and Jel]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He pronounced</hi> (Er-Rághib, K) a thing <hi rend="ital">by a true judgment</hi> or <hi rend="ital">decision,</hi> (Er-Rághib,) or <hi rend="ital">as a legal ordinance;</hi> (K;) as in the saying (of the Legislator, TA), <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَ ٱللّٰهُ الصَّلَوَاتِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">المَفْرُوضَاتِ خَمْسًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">God hath pronounced the prayers that are made obligatory to be five</hi>] (K.) And <hi rend="ital">He pronounce</hi> (Er-Rághib, K *) a thing <hi rend="ital">by a false judgment</hi> or <hi rend="ital">decision,</hi> (Er-Rághib,) or <hi rend="ital">according to his own judgment, heretically;</hi> (K;) as in the saying [in the Kur xv. 91], <foreign lang="ar">الَّذِينَ جَعَلُوا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">القُرْآنَ عِضِينَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Who pronounced the Kur-án to be lies,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">enchantment,</hi> &amp;c.]. (Er-Rághib, K.)          <sense type="b" n="9">-b9-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He called,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">named,</hi> (S, Msb, K,) a thing; (Msb;) as in the saying [in the Kur xliii. 18], <foreign lang="ar">وَجَعَلُوا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">المَلَائِكَةَ الَّذِينَ هُمْ عِبَادُ الرَّحْمٰنِ إِنَاثًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And they have called the angels, who are the servants of the Compassionate, females</hi>]: (S, K:) or, as some say, the meaning is, <hi rend="ital">have described them as, and pronounced them to be, females;</hi> like as one says, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَ فُلَانٌ زَيْدًا أَعْلَمَ النَّاسِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Such a one described Zeyd as, and pronounced him to be, the most learned of men</hi>]: or <hi rend="ital">have held,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">believed, them to be females;</hi> like as the verb signifies in the saying in the Kur [xvi. 59], <foreign lang="ar">وَيَجْعَلُونَ لِلّٰهِ البَنَاتِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And they hold,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">believe, God to have daughters:</hi> or this may be rendered <hi rend="ital">and they attribute to God daughters</hi>]. (TA.) You say also, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلْتُ زَيْدًا أَخَاكَ</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">I asserted Zeyd to be related to thee</hi> [<hi rend="ital">as a brother;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I called Zeyd thy brother</hi>]. (K.)          <sense type="b" n="10">-b10-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He thought;</hi> as in the saying, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلَ البَصْرَةَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بَغْدَادَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He thought El-Basrah to be Baghdád</hi>]; (K;) and so in the saying, <foreign lang="ar">جَعَلْتُهُ عَبْدًا فَشَتَمْتُهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I thought him to be a slave, and consequently I reviled him</hi>].
